 bharat kaa samvidhan samvidhan sabha dwaara 26 navambar 1949 ko paarit hua tathaa 26 janvari 1950 se prabhavi hua
 The Constitution of India is the largest written constitution in the world
 isamen ab 450 anuchhed, tathaa 12 anusuchiyaan hai or ye 22 bhaagon main vibhajit he
 Some of these important paragraphs are the following: 1
 anuchhed 1 :yah ghoshnaa karata he ki bharat rajyon kaa sangh he
 2
 anuchhed 3:sansad vidhi dwaara nae rajya bana sakati he tathaa pehle se avasthit rajyon ke kshetron, simaaon evam naamon main parivartan kar sakati he
 3
 anuchhed 5:samvidhan ke prarambh hone ke, samay bharat main rahane vaale ve sabhi vyakti yahaan ke naagarik honge, jinka janm bharat main hua ho, jinke pita yaa mata bharat ke naagarik hon yaa samvidhan ke prarambh ke samay se bharat main rah rahe hon
 4
 anuchhed 53:sangh kii karypalika sambandhi shakti raashtrapati main nihit rahegi
 5

 dam main kariban 7
 5 lakh cusecs of water has increased
